                                                    <div class="ep-card__body">
                                                                                                        <p class="ep-text mb-2">
                                        Carey Price plays the butterfly-style close to perfection. Has very good size for a goaltender in today’s game and combined with his athleticism and almost flawless lateral movement it will need a deflection or a perfect shot to beat him. An excellent stick- and puckhandler, Carey Price can support his defense with either crisp and long outlet-passes or just clearing the puck out of the zone. Has tremendous ability to read the game and seems to always stay composed in hectic situations and always has track of the puck which gives him excellent rebound control. Can win games single handedly, when standing on his head in big games. (by Rafik Soliman, October 2014)<br>
<br>
Father: <a href="/player.php?player=48278">Jerry Price</a><br>
Cousin: <a href="/player.php?player=9333">Keaton Ellerby</a><br>
Second cousin: <a href="/player.php?player=9137">Shane Doan</a>
                                    </p>
                                                                                                                                </div>

    <component is="script" >        $(function() {
            $('.daterange').daterangepicker({
                'linkedCalendars': false,
                'showCustomRangeLabel': false,
                                                'opens': 'center',
                'drops': 'auto',
                'locale': { 'cancelLabel': 'Clear' },
            }, function (start, end, label) {
                let container = $('#game-logs');
                $('input[name="from"]', container).val(start.format('YYYY-MM-DD'));
                $('input[name="to"]', container).val(end.format('YYYY-MM-DD'));
                changeGameLogsFilter();
            }).on('cancel.daterangepicker', function(ev, picker) {
                let container = $('#game-logs');
                $('input[name="from"]', container).val('');
                $('input[name="to"]', container).val('');
                changeGameLogsFilter();
            });

            $('.daterange-opener').click(function() {
                $('.daterange').click();
            });
        });
    </component>                    </div>

                navigator.serviceWorker.register('https://static.eliteprospects.com/sw.js?v=3246').then(function(registration) {
                    // Registration was successful
                    console.log('ServiceWorker registration successful with scope: ', registration.scope);
                }, function(err) {
                    // registration failed :(
                    console.log('ServiceWorker registration failed: ', err);
                });
            });
        }
    </script>
